%\begin{multicols}{2}
\begin{center}
{\huge\bfseries anubaMdha 1}

\smallskip

{\huge\bfseries hecicxna pAriBASika padagaLu}
\end{center}

\medskip

\begin{entry}
\word{aMgasathxla-liMgasathxla saMbaMdha}
\meaning{\arthanonum{parashivanu mAnava matutx parxpaMcavanunx saqSiTxmADida meVle adariMda dUra uLiyade, adaralelxV aMtagaRtanAgirutAtxne. manuSayxnu parashivananunx Aru sathxlagaLalilx sAkASxtAkxra mADikoLaLxbahudu. aMgana I Aru aMgasathxlagaLeMdare Bakatx, maheVsha, parxsAdi, pArxNaliMgi, sharaNa matutx aikayx. avanu sAkASxtAkxra mADikoLuLxva shivana sathxlagaLige liMgasathxlaveMba hesaridudx, avu karxmavAgi AcAra\-liMga, guruliMga, shivaliMga, jaMgamaliMga, parxsAdaliMga matutx mahAliMga enisikoLuLxtatxve. I Aru aMgasathxlagaLu\break Aru liMgasathxlagaLalilx saMbaMdha hoMdive. heVgeMdare: \hbox{manuSayxna} aMgavu parashivana shakitxya rUpAMtara. \hbox{manuSayxnu} baMdhanadalilxruvavarege aMgasathxlagaLu shakitx athavA adhoVmAye enisikoLuLxtatxve. oMdu veVLe avanu avugaLanunx AdhAyxtimxka udedxVshakAkxgi baLasidare avu Bakitx athavA UdhavxRmAye enisikoLuLxtatxve.}}
\vskip 4pt
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad motatxmodalaneya AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya haMtadalilxruva sAdhaka BakatxnenisikoLuLxtAtxne. \hbox{parashivana} kirxyAshakitxyu\break Bakatxnalilx GArxNeVMdirxyavAgi rUpAMtaragoMDidudx adaralilx\break \hbox{parashivanu} AcAraliMgarUpadalilx aMtagaRtavAgidAdxne. AcAra\-liMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxbeVkeMba Bakatxnu tananx citatxvanenxV hasatx\-vanAnxgi mADikoMDu AcAraliMgakekx parimaLadarxvayxgaLanunx apiRsutAtxne hAgU A apiRtavu gaMdhaveMba parxsAdavAgutatxde. Bakatxna I Bakitxge vishAvxsaBakitx athavA sharxdAdhxBakitx athavA\break sadaBxkitx eMdu hesaru. hiVge apiRsida citatxvu sucitatxvenisi\-koLuLxtatxde. GArxNeVMdirxyadalilxruva AcAraliMgakekx avanu apiRsuvudariMda, GArxNeVMdirxyavu (mUgu) parashivana (AcAraliMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde.}}
\medskip
\begin{shl}
AcArAyApiRtA paqthivxV guroVrApaH samapiRtAH\\[2pt]
shivAya cApiRtaM teVjashacxrAya marudapiRtaH\\[2pt]
parxsAdAyApiRtaM voyxVma jiVvAtAmx mahateV\char'263piRtaH~ BajeVta\\[-1pt]
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(a.sU., 7.45)}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya eraDaneya haMtadalilxruva \hbox{sAdhakanige} maheVsha (mAheVshavxra) eMdu hesaru. parashivana jAcnxna\-shakitxyu mAheVshasathxladalilxruva sAdhakanalilx jihevxVMdirxya\-vAgi (nAlageyAgi) rUpAMtaragoMDidudx, parashivanu adaralilx guru\-liMga\-vAgi aMtagaRtavAgidAdxne. guruliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxbeVkeMba maheVshanu tananx budidhxyanenxV hasatx\-vanAnxgi mADikoMDu, rasaveMba darxvayxvanunx apiRsi, adanunx ruciyeMba parxsAdavanAnxgi mADikoLuLxtAtxne. maheVshana I Bakitxge neYSiThxkaBakitx eMdu hesaru. rasavanunx apiRsuva maheVshana budidhxge subudidhxyeMdu hesaru. nAlageyalilxruva guruliMgakekx\break avanu ruciyanunx apiRsuvudariMda, A apaRNeyanunx sivxVkari\-suva jihevxVMdirxyavu (nAlageyu) parashivana (guru\-liMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde.}}
\medskip
\begin{shl}
AcAreV divayxliMgeV nirupamanijaBakatxsathxlAMgeYkayxBAji\\[2pt]
GArxNAKeyxV citatxhasetxVna ca GanasuKaheVtw kirxyAshakitxyuketxV\\[2pt]
GArxtavayxM darxvayxmapayxpaRNaviSayavidhAnoVpadiSaTxM samapayxR\\[2pt]
pArxyasasxdaBxkitxpUNaR savxyamayamiha gaMdha parxsAdaM~ BajeVta\\[-1pt]
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(a.sU., 7.46)}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya mUraneya haMtadalilxruva sAdhaka\-nige parxsAdi eMdu hesaru. parashivana icACxshakitxyu \hbox{sAdhakana} neVtarxvAgi rUpAMtaragoMDidudx, adaralilx aMtasathxvAgiruva parashivanige shivaliMga eMdu hesaru. shivaliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisi\-koLaLxbeVkeMba parxsAdiyu tananx ahaMkAra\-vanenxV hasatxvanAnxgi mADikoMDu rUpadarxvayxgaLanunx shiva\-liMgakekx apiRsi, adanunx rUpa eMba parxsAdavanAnxgi mADikoLuLxtAtxne. \hbox{parxsAdiya} I Bakitxge avadhAnaBakitx eMdu hesaru.\break beLakanunx apiRsuva parxsAdiya ahaMkArakekx nirahaMkAraveMdu hesaru. neVtarx\-dalilxruva shivaliMgakekx avanu rUpavanunx apiRsu\-vuda\-riMda A apaRNeyanunx sivxVkarisuva neVterxVMdirxyavu (kaNuNx) parashivana (shivaliMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde.}}
\medskip
\begin{shl}
sAvxMgeV mAheVshavxrAtamxnayxnupamasahajajAcnxnashakitxparxyuketxV\\[2pt]
jihAvxseyxV suparxsidedhxV parataraguruliMgABidheV saMsithxteV\char'263simxnf\\[2pt]
niSAThxBakitxparxBAvaparxNihitasumahAbudidhxhasetxVna vidAvxnf\\[2pt]
rasayxM darxvayxM samapayxR savxyamamalarasAKayxM parxsAdaM~ BajeVta\\[-1pt]
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(a.sU., 7.47)}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad AdhAyxtimxka sAdhaneya nAlakxneya haMtadalilxruva sAdhaka\-nige pArxNaliMgiyeMdu hesaru. parashivana Adishakitxyu \hbox{sAdhakana} tavxgiMdirxyavAgi rUpAMtaragoMDidudx, adaralilx aMtasathx\-vAgiruva parashivanige jaMgamaliMgaveMdu hesaru. jaMgamaliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxbeVkeMba pArxNaliMgiyu\break tananx manasasxnenxV hasatxvanAnxgi mADikoMDu, sapxshaRdarxvayxgaLanunx jaMgama\-liMgakekx apiRsi, adanunx sapxshaRveMba parxsAdavanAnxgi mADikoLuLxtAtxne. pArxNaliMgiya I Bakitxge anuBAvaBakitx eMdu hesaru. sapxshaRvanunx apiRsuva pArxNaliMgiya manasisxge\break sumanaveMdu hesaru. tavxgiMdirxya (camaR) dalilxruva jaMgama\-liMgakekx avanu soVMkanunx apiRsuvudariMda, adanunx sivxVkari\-suva tavxgiMdirxyavu parashivana (jaMgamaliMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisi\-koLuLxtatxde.}}
\medskip
\begin{shl}
yoV\char'263sw nitayxM parxsAdisathxlaparamapadapArxpatxdivAyxMgaBAji\\[2pt]
sevxVcACxshakitxparxyuketx daqshi jagati muKeV pANinA\char'263haMkaqteVna\\[2pt]
sAkASxlilxMgeV shivAKeyxV savinayamavadhAnAtamxtABakitxyukotxV\\[2pt]
darxSaTxvAyxMtaM samapAyxRpaRNavinihitarUpaparxsAdaM~ BajeVta\\[-1pt]
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(a.sU., 7.48)}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad aidaneya haMtadalilxruva sAdhakanige sharaNaneMdu hesaru. parashivana parAshakitxyu sharaNana shorxVterxVMdirxyavAgi rUpAMtara\-goMDidudx, adaralilx aMtasathxvAgiruva parashivanige parxsAda\-liMgaveMdu hesaru. parxsAdaliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisi\-koLaLx\-beVkeMba sharaNanu tananx jAcnxnavanenxV hasatxvanAnxgi mADikoMDu, shabadxvanunx parxsAdaliMgakekx apiRsi, sushabadxveMdu parxsAda\-vanunx paDeyutAtxne. sharaNana I Bakitxge AnaMdaBakitx eMdu hesaru. shabadxvanunx apiRsuvudariMda, A apaRNeyanunx sivxVkarisuva shorxVterxVMdirxyavu parashivana (parxsAda\-liMgada) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde.}}
\medskip
\begin{shl}
saMsaketxV pArxNaliMgisathxlanihitanijAMgeV manaHpANinA\char'263sw\\[2pt]
liMgeV sAkASxcaCxrAKeyxV tavxci jagati muKeV hAyxdishakitxparxyuketxV\\[2pt]
sapxrXSaTxvayxM cApaRyitAvx savxyamanuBavaBakitxparxBAvoVpapanonxV\\[2pt]
nitayxM sapxshaRparxsAdaM niratishayasuKaM tatatxvXveVtAtx~ BajeVta\\[-1pt]
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(a.sU., 7.49)}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad koneya haMtada sAdhakanige aikayxneMdu hesaru. \hbox{parashivana} citfshakitxyu aikayxna BAva(haqdaya)vAgi rUpAMtara\break\-goMDidudx, adaralilx aMtasathxvAgiruva parashivanige mahA\-liMga\-veMdu hesaru. mahAliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxbeVkeMba aikayxnu tananx BAvavanenxV (jiVvAtamxnanenxV) hasatxvanAnxgi mADikoLuLxtAtxne. aikayxnu toVrisuva Bakitxge samarasaBakitx eMdu\break hesaru. taqpitxyanunx apiRsuva aikayxna BAvakekx kelavu veVLe sadABxva\-veMdu kareyalAgutatxde. haqdayadalilxruva mahA\-liMgakekx avanu taqpitxyanunx apiRsuvudariMda, A apaRNe\-yanunx sivxVkarisuva haqdayavu parashivana (mahAliMgana) bAyi (muKa) enisikoLuLxtatxde.}}
\medskip
\begin{shl}
liMgeV sAkASxtapxrXsAdeV vimalasharaNasaMjAcnxMgasaMsAthxpiteV\char'263simxnf\\[2pt]
shorxVtavayxM shorxVtarxvaketxrXV niKilamiha parAshakitxyuketxV samapayxR\\[2pt]
AnaMdAkAraBakitx suPxTataraparamajAcnxnahasetxVna soV\char'263yaM\\[2pt]
shabAhxKayxM tatapxrXsAdaM savxyamaviratamatAyxsharxmasothxV~ BajeVta\\[-1pt]
\end{shl}
\medskip
\pauthor{(a.sU., 7.50)}

%\artha{aikayxsathxla, AcArasaMpatitxsathxla, EkaBAjanasathxla matutx sahaBoVjanasathxla eMba 4 viBAgagaLu aikayxsathxladalilxve.}}

\begin{entry}
\word{arivu kuruhu}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{tiLivaLike; I iMdirxyagoVcara vishiSaTx jAcnxna; arivu uMTAguvudu citfdalilx moVha, ahaMkAra, loVBAdi guNagaLu BAvarUpadalilx nelasidare `citf'ge ashudadhx\-BAvagaLa leVpanavuMTAgi aviveVka Avarisutatxde. jiVvAtamxnu liMgavanunx kuruhu (saMkeVta) mADikoMDu sAdhanegeYdare ashudadhx\-BAva ilalxvAgutatxde:}
\ullekha{nenahu satitxtutx BArxMtu beMditutx arivu mareyitutx kuruhugeTiTxtutx (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 298-86); ariyade ajAcnxnadalilx kuruhu bididxtetxMdu pArxNAGAtava mADikoMDu sAva ajAcnxnigaLa noVDA! (savasaM.\break 3; cenanxba. 1275-449); neleya meVliTuTx kuruhu\-geDabalalxDe terahilalx kapilasidadhxmalilxkAjuRna (savasaM. 4; sidadhxrA. 701-198).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{apiRtavilalxda ApAyxyini}
\meaning{\arthanonum{shivanalilx oMdAgiruva GanavAda taqpitx; liMga aMga beVreyeMdukoMDa\-vanu liMgakekx (parashiva\-nige) halavu BakaSxyXBoVjayxgaLanunx apiRsi, avugaLanunx parxsAda\-veMdu sivxVkarisi taqpitxpaDutAtxne. Adare, liMgAnuBAviyAda\break sharaNanu EnanUnx liMgakekx apiRsa\-deyeV, EnanUnx parxsAda\-veMdu sivxVkarisadeyeV taqpitxpaTuTx\-koLuLxtAtxne:} \ullekha{kamaR\-vilalxda kAraNi\-kanu, apiRtavilalxda ApAyxyani, jaMgamavilalxda sama\-shiVlanu, liMgavilalxda nirutanu (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 759-226).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{asaMKAyxta(ru)}
\meaning{\arthanonum{shivaBakatx; sharaNaru:}
\ullekha{toreyudakava kereyuMDu taqpatxvAgalu A kereyudakava halavu kelavu sAthxvara jaMgamagaLuMDu taqpitxvaDevaMte, parxBudeVvara taqpitx asaMKAyxta mahAgaNaMgaLelalxkekx taqpitxyAyitutx noVDA (savasaM. 1; basava. 1210-333); anaMtaloVkAloVkada asaMKAyxta mahAgaNaMgaLelalxru liMgaBAvadalilx BaritarAgi, gaganasidAdhxMtadiMda upa\-deVshakekx baMdu BakitxrAjayxvane hokukx, nijaliMgasukeSxVtarxvane kaMDu, aKaMDa paripUNaR pUjeya mADuvavarige namoVnamoV eMbe guheVshavxrA (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 281-82); iSaTx pArxNa BAvaveMba tirxvidhaliMgasaMbaMdha beVDaveMdaDe asaMKAyxta parxmathagaNaMgaLopupxvare? kUDalacenanxsaMgayayxnalilx iSaTxliMgasaMbaMdhavilalxdavara muKava noVDalAgadu parxBuve (savasaM. 3; cenanxba.\break 1642-600); basavaNaNx, kapilasidadhxmalilxkAjuRnA, cenanx\-basavaNaNx\-nAgi parxBu modalAgi asaMKAyxtarelalxranu toVride guruve (savasaM. 4; sidadhxrA. 1323-382); tanu shudadhx\-vAyitutx shivaBakatxrokukxda koMDenanx. mana shudadhxvAyitutx\break asaMKAyxtara nenedenanx kaMgaLu shudadhxvAyitutx sakalagaNaMgaLa noVDi enanx (savasaM. 5; akakxma. 230-69); ele asaMKAyxtarira I huyayxlanavadharisi salahi (basapu. 44-48).}}
\vskip 5pt
\newmeaning{\ni{na saMKAyxtaM - asaMKAyxtaM}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{asaMsAkxra}
\meaning{\arthanonum{viVrasheYva diVkeSxyanunx paDeyadavanu:} \ullekha{atapatxtanu\-rajojxV veY AmaH saMsAkxravajiRtaH. viVrasheYva diVkeSxyanunx \hbox{paDeyade} berasidene BaviBeVda uLidanukarisi keYkoMDene \hbox{asaMsAkxra} racita pAkaMgaLaM parihariseneV (basapu. 44-15).}}
\vskip 5pt
\newmeaning{\ni{avidayxmAnaH saMsAkxroV yasayx|}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{aLimana}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{asithxra manasusxLaLxvanu:} \ullekha{kUDalasaMgama\-deVvara Bakitx aLimanadavarige aLavaDadayAyx (savasaM. 1; basava. 668-167).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{aLivu}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{liMgAMgasAmarasayxvanunx sAdhisi matetx huTaTxdiruvudu:} \ullekha{aLivarige uLivu elilxyU ilalxveMdu tiLi, uLivarige aLivu elilxyU ilalxveMdu tiLi (savasaM. 8; moVLige. 1490-500).}}
\end{entry}

\meaning{\arthanonum{Agasa; gagana; paMcamahABUtagaLalilx hAgU \hbox{mUvatAtxru} tatatxvXgaLalilx
oMdu; shabadxvu guNavU vAyxpakavU Adudu. elalx jiVvarAshigaLige avakAsha
niVDiruvudariMda AkAsha eniside. elalx iMdirxyagaLige avakAsha niVDiruvudariMda
upAdhi\-BeVdadiMda haqdayAkAsha eniside. AkAshavu budidhxtatatxvXkekx mUla AdhAra:}}

\newmeaning{\ullekha{paqthivx apupx teVja vAyu AkAsha niraMjanadeVvA nimamx mahimeya parxNavasavxrUpaMgalalxde kANalArigeyU bAradayAyx (savasaM. 1; basava. 814-209); sadoyxVjAtamuKadalilx paqthivx puTiTxtutx, ...IshAnamuKadalilx AkAsha puTiTxtutx; iMtiV paMcabarxhamxdiMda paMcamahABUtaMgaLu huTiTxduvu... AkAshakekx shabadx oMdeV guNa bayali\-gihude dhamaR suLihudakekx te\char'273huguDuvude kamaR kaqSaNxvaNaR adhideVvate sadAshivanu (karaha. 658-7).}}

\begin{entry}
\word{AkAshada pUvARsharxya}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{\hbox{paMcaBUtagaLalolxMdAda} AkAshatatatxvXkekx shabadxveV muKayx guNa. namamx deVhadalilx AkAshatatatxvXviruvudariMda namage shabadx keVLisutatxde. sharaNanu tAnu keVLisikoMDududelalx shivamaMtarxveMdu managANutAtxne. idariMdAgi AkAshatatatxvXvu tananx pUvARsharxyavanunx kaLedukoMDu, AdhAyxtimxka parxgatige sAdhanavAgutatxde:} \ullekha{Bakatx Bakatx\-neMbaru, paqthivxya pUvARsharxyava kaLeyalariyadananxkakx ...AkAshada pUvAR\break\-sharxyava kaLeyalariyadananxkakx... BakatxreMdu liMgava pUjisu\-vavara kaMDu nAnu beragAde guheVshavxra (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 136-42); AkAshada pUvARsharxya maMtarxdiMda hoVhudu (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 47-15).}}
\vskip 5pt
\newmeaning{\ni{pUvaRshacx asw Asharxyashacx - pUvARsharxyaH}}

\meaning{\arthanonum{nAvu yAvoMdu vasutx athavA GaTaneyanunx noVDidarU adakokxMdu kAraNa\-viraleV\-beVku enunxtetxVve. kAraNa yAvudeMdu namage sadayxkekx gotitxlalx\-dirabahudu, Adare kAraNavilalxda GaTanegaLilalx. adeV riVti yAvudeV oMdu GaTaneyanunx noVDidarU, idakekx kAyaR (pariNAma) iraleVbeVku eMdukoLuLxtetxVve. adara pariNAma\-gaLu namage sadayxkekx gotitxlalxdirabahudu. Adare pariNAma\-vilalxda GaTanegaLilalx.}}
\vskip 4pt
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad saqSiTx mADabeVkeMba iceCx parashivanalilx inUnx mUDade idAdxga aMdare, parashivanu shUnayxsithxtiyalilxdAdxga, avanu kAyaRnU alalx, kAraNanU alalx. saqSiTxsilalxvAdudariMda avanu kAyaRnalalx enunxvudeVnoV sariyeV. \vskip 4pt
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\qquad parashiva inUnx shUnayxsithxtiyalilxruvAga avanu saqSiTxkataR (kAraNa), jagatutx pariNAma eMdu heVLalu baruvudilalx. saqSiTxyAda meVle I BeVda sAdhayxveV horatu, saqSiTxpUvaRdalilx sAdhayxvilalx. \ullekha{ayayx! kAyaRnalalx kAraNanalalx noVDa! niravaya\-shUnayxliMgamUtiR... iMdu uBayavaLidu beLaguva saMgana\-basavaNaNxna unamxnAgarxdali hoLevAta tAne noVDA! guheVshavxraliMgavu cenanxbasavaNaNx (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 781-218);\break kAyaRnalalx kAraNanalalx kalipxtanalalx, niviRkalipxtanalalx, nenahu\-mAtarxdiMda jagava saqSiTxsideneMba BAva baNiteyavanalalx, idiriMge tAnilalx, tanage idirAgi oMdu vasutxvilalx, parxtiyilalxdaparxtima, anupama\-mahima, ninanx niHkalaneMdeMbarayAyx, mahAliMgaguru shivasidedhxVshavxraparxBuveV (savasaM. 11; toVMTasi. 25-11).}}
\vskip 5pt
\newmeaning{\arthanonum{\SEE{Adi anAdi ilalxdaMdu}}}
\end{entry}

\meaning{\arthanonum{sadoyxVjAta, vAmadeVva, aGoVra, tatupxruSa matutx IshAnareV paMcabarxhamxru. vAsatxvika\-vAgi ivaru shivana aidu  rUpa\-gaLu; shivaniMda huTiTxda I paMcabarxhamxru vishavxvanUnx  mAnavanige beVkAda deVheVMdirxyAdigaLanUnx saqSiTxsalu beVkAda  upAdAnakAraNavAda paMcaBUtagaLanunx saqSiTxsutAtxre. athavA kelavu  vacanakArara parxkAra shivashakitxya aidu rUpagaLAda aidu  BUtagaLige I paMca\-barxhamxru adhideVvate\-gaLu. aMdare,  paMcaBUtagaLiMdAda deVhavanunx saqSiTxsidudakekx nAvu I  paMcabarxhamxrige QuNigaLAgirabeVku. I athaRdalilx namamxlilxruva  paqthivx aMshavu adara adhi\-deVvateyAda sadoyxVjAtana haMgu, adeV  riVti jalavu vAmadeVvana, aginxyu aGoVrana, vAyuvu tatupxruSana hAgU AkAshavu IshAnana haMgu. I deVha namamxdalalx, parashivanu namage koTiTxruva sAla eMbudu idara athaR. I sAlavanunx nAvu Bakitx matutx nisAvxthaR\-teya mUlaka tiVrisabeVku:}
\ullekha{paqthivx sadoyxVjAtana haMgu, jala vAmadeVvana haMgu, aginx aGoVrana haMgu, vAyu tatupxruSana haMgu, AkAsha IshAnana haMgu, paMcabarxhamxva maredu, OMkAra barxhamx\-vanari aiGaTa dUra rAmeVshavxraliMgava (savasaM. 8; meremiM. 1354-464).}}

 naDeyuvudu muMtAda kirxyegaLu vAyuvina pariNAmagaLu.}

\begin{entry}
\word{parxNavadaAkaqtigaLu}
\src{va}
\meaning{\artha{parxNavaveMdare, OM namaH shivAya eMba Aru akaSxrada maMtarx I maMtarxda akaSxragaLu karxmavAgi tAraka, daMDaka, kuMDala, adhaRcaMdarx, dapaRNa, joyxVti-ya AkAravuLaLxvugaLAgive:} \ullekha{inunx parxNavada lakaSxNavadeMteMdaDe: parxthama tAraka savxrUpavAgihudu. divxtiVya daMDasavxrUpavAgihudu. taqtiVya kuMDalAkAravAgihudu. catuthaR adhaRcaMdarxkAkAravAgihudu. paMcama dapaRNAkAravAgihudu. SaSaThx joyxVtisavxrUpavAgihudu noVDA. idakekx IshavxroVvAca: ``parxthamaM tArakA\-rUpaM| divxtiVyaM daMDa ucayxteV| taqtiVyaM kuMDalAkAraM| catuthaR cAdhaRcaMdarxkaM|| paMcamaM dapaRNAkAraM| SaSaThx joyxVtisavxrUpakaM| iti parxNava vijecnxVyaM| yadogxVpayxM varAnaneV||" iMteMdudAgi, aparxmANakUDalasaMgamadeVvA (savasaM. 13; bAlasaM. 501-252).} \artha{paqthivx, apupx(jala), teVjasusx, vAyu, AkAsha, AtamxgaLu karxmavAgi parxNavada tAraka, daMDaka, kuMDala, adhaRcaMdarx, dapaRNa, joyxVti savxrUpagaLalilx nelesive:}
\ullekha{matatxM, A shiSayxnu ele sadugxrusAvxmi, aKaMDajoyxVtimaRyavAgiha paramoVMkAra utapxtayxvanu nimamx mahAvAkayxdiMda nirUpisi, nimamx sAvxnuBAvadaqkikxniMda toVralu kaMDu suKiyAdenu. inunx SaDivxdha BUtaMgaLutapxtayx nAyxsasathxlavanu nirUpiseMdu binenxYsalu, A sadugxrusAvxmi nirUpisidaradeMteMdaDe: aKaMDajoyxVtimaRyavAgiha paramoVMkAra parxNavada joyxVtisavxrUpadalilx AtamxnutapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada dapaRNAkAradalilx AkAsha utapxtayxvAyitutx. A parxNavada adhaRcaMdArxkAdalilx vAyu utapxtayxvAyitutx. A parxNavada kuMDalAkAradalilx teVja utapxtayxvAyitutx. A parxNavada daMDakasavxrUpadalilx apupx utapxtayxvAyitutx. A parxNavada tArakasavxrUpadalilx paqthivx utapxtayxvAyitutx noVDA. idakekx citapxrXkAshAgameV: ``OMkAra joyxVtirUpeV ca| AtAmx ceYva samudaBxvaH| OMkAra dapaRNAkAreV| AkAshaM ca samudaBxvaM|| OMkAreV cAdhaRcaMderxV ca| vAyushecxYva samudaBxvaH| OMkAra kuMDalAkAreV| teVjashecxYva samudaBxvaM|| OMkAra daMDarUpeV ca| ApashecxYva samudaBxvaH| OMkAra tArakarUpeV| paqthivxshacx samudaBxvaH| iti SaSaThxBUtaM deVviV| sAthxna sAthxneV samudaBxma||" iMteMdudAgi, aparxmANakUDalasaMgamadeVvA (savasaM. 13; bAlasaM. 502-253); A aKaMDa joyxVtimaRya\-vAgiha paramoVMkAraparxNavada tArakAsavxrUpadalilx paqthivxyeMba mahA\-BUtavihudu. A parxNavada daMDasavxrUpadalilx apupxveMba mahABUtavihudu. A parxNavada kuMDalAkAradalilx teVjaveMba mahABUtavihudu. A parxNavada adhaRcaMdarxkadalilx vAyuveMba mahABUtavihudu. A parxNavada dapaRNAkAradalilx AkAshaveMba mahABUtavihudu. A parxNavada joyxVtisavxrUpadalilx AtamxneMba mahABUtavihudu noVDA. idakekx citipxMDAgameV: ``OMkAra tArakarUpeV| paqthivxBUtaM samAcareVtf| OMkAra daMDarUpeV ca| apupx BUta samAshirxtAH|| OMkAra kuMDalAkAreV| teVja\-BUtaH tathABaveVtf| OMkAra adhaRcaMderxV ca| vAyuBUtaM ca vataRteV|| OMkAra dapaRNAkAreV| voyxVmaBUtaM sadAshirxtAH| OMkAra joyxVtirUpeV ca| AtamxBUtAshirxtaM tathA| iti SaSaThxBUtaM deVviV| sAthxna sAthxneV samAcareVtf||" iMteMdudAgi. aparxmANakUDalasaMgamadeVvA (savasaM. 13; bAlasaM. 503-254).} \artha{Bakatx, maheVshavxra, parxsAdi, pArxNaliMgi, sharaNa, aikayx - ivarugaLu tAraka, daMDaka, kuMDala, adhaRcaMdarx, dapaRNa, joyxVti savxrUpagaLiMda karxmavAgi udaBxvisidaru:} \ullekha{matatxM, A shiSayxnu ele sadugxrusAvxmi, SaDivxdhaBUtaMgaLutapxtayx nAyxsasathxlavanu nimamx mahAnuBAvavacanadiMda nirUpisi, nimamx mahAnuBAvadaqkikxniMda toVralu, kaMDu paramasuKiyAdenu. inunx BakatxmAheVshavxra parxsAdi pArxNaliMgi sharaNa aikayxrutapxtayx nAyxsa sathxlavanu nirUpiseMdu binenxYsalu, A sadugxrusAvxmi nirUpisidaradeMteMdaDe: aKaMDa joyxVtimaRyavAgiha paramoVMkAra parxNavada joyxVtisavxrUpadalilx aikayxnutapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada dapaRNAkAradalilx sharaNanutapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada adhaRcaMdarxkadalilx pArxNaliMgi utapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada kuMDalAkAradalilx parxsAdi utapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada daMDakasavxrUpadalilx maheVshavxra utapxtayxvAdanu. A parxNavada tArakasavxrUpadalilx BakatxnutapxtayxvAdanu noVDA. idakekx citapxrXkAshAgamoVtatxrasAreV: ``OMkAra joyxVtirUpeV ca| aikayxMtu samu\-daBxvaM| OMkAra dapaRNAkAreV| sharaNashacx samudaBxvaM|| OMkAreVcAdhaRcaMderxV ca| pArxNaliMgiV samudaBxvaM|| OMkAra kuMDalAkAreV| parxsAdiVshacx samudaBxvaM|| OMkAra daMDakarUpeV ca| mAheVshavxra samudaBxvaH| OMkAra tArakA\-rUpeV| BakatxshecxYva samudaBxvaH| iti SaDusathxlaM deVviV| sAthxnasAthxneVSu jAyateV|| iMteMdudAgi, aparxmANakUDalasaMgamadeVvA (\hbox{savasaM.} 13; bAlasaM. 504-254).}}
\end{entry}

\meaning{\arthanonum{viVrasheYva sidAdhxMtadaMte deVhada benunxhuri, kutitxge, BUrxmadhayx matutx netitxyalilx parashiva nelesirutAtxne. mUlAdhAradalilxruva shivanige AcAraliMgaveMdu hesaru. shivanu citfsavxrUpanAdudariMda, avanu nelesalu athavA vayxkatxvAgalu oMdu mAdhayxma beVku. kirxyAshakitxyeV A mAdhayxma. kirxyAshakitx paqthivxV BUtada matotxMdu hesaru. adara adhideVvate AcAraliMga.}}
\smallskip

\begin{entry}
\word{madhayxmada suKa}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{BUmiyalilxna suKa; pArxpaMcika suKa; BUmi, savxgaR matutx pAtakada madhayxdalilxruvudariMda pArxpaMcika suKa:} \ullekha{madhayxmada suKavanu hodudxva tatavxvanu adhaRbiMbagaLa kiraNaMgaLa I hodadxda parxpaMcikava nitayxda tatavxvanu madhayxmadalilx kaMDe kANA kapilasidadhxmalilxkAjuRna (savasaM. 4; sidadhxrA. 873-246).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{anuBAviyU liMgAMga sAmarasayxdiMdAgi tananxtanavanunx kaLedu koLuLxtAtxne. avanu yoVcisuvudu, iciCxsuvudu, elalxvU \hbox{shivana} iceCxyiMdaleV horatu, taninxceCxyiMdalalx:}
\ullekha{ayAyx, nimamx anuBAvadiMda enanx mana hALAyitatxyAyx (savasaM. 1; basava. 509-123).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{manadasUtaka hiMgisuvudu}

uLida nAlukx guNagaLU, aginxge shabadx, sapxshaR matutx rUpa (teVja)
eMba mUru guNagaLU, vAyuvige shabadx matutx sapxshaRveMba eraDu
guNagaLU, AkAshakekx shabadxveMba oMdeV guNavU ide.}}

\meaning{\arthanonum{jAcnxnaveMba beLakanunx pUje matitxtara kirxyegaLiMda noVDalu sAdhayx\-vilalx. adakekx sAvxnuBAva Avashayxka. kirxyegaLu namamxnunx sAtivxkaranAnxgi mADadidadxre sAvxnuBAva sAdhayxvilalx. sAvxnuBAvadalilx nAvu kANuva beLagu horaginadalalx, namamxlelxV avayxkatxvAgiruva beLaku:}
\ullekha{sharaNatatigaLiMda karaNaMgaLa nivArisi iMtapapx kirxyApUje, bAhayxda sharxdedhx, jAcnxnada beLagu, sAvxnuBAva sananxdadhx (savasaM 5, moVLige 946-302).}}
\end{entry}


\begin{entry}
\word{sidadhxparxsAdiya aMga}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{jAcnxneVMdirxya, kameRVMdirxya matutx aMtaHkaraNagaLa saluvAgi sharaNanu parxsAdavanunx sivxVkarisade elalxvU shivana parxsAdaveMdU adu jAcnxneVMdirxyAdigaLanunx shudadhxmADutatxdeMdU tiLidu sivxVkarisidare aMthavana aMgavu sidadhxparxsAdiya aMgavenisikoLuLxtatxde. sidadhxparxsAdiyu parxpaMcadalilx parashivana parxsAdavananxlalxde matetxVnanUnx kANuvudilalx. avanu noVDuva noVTa, kANuva rUpu, keVLuva shabadx elalxvU avana parxkAra shivana parxsAdaveV:}
\ullekha{karaNaMgaLicecxyilalxde koMbudu sidadhxparxsAdiya aMga (savasaM. 8, parxleMbaM. 118-48).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{suKava nishecxYsuvudu}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{nishecxYsuvudu eMbudanunx sAdhisuvudu, sAkASxtakxrisikoLuLxvudu eMba athaRdalilx baLasalAgide. suMkada baMkaNaNxnu `suKavanunx nishecxYsalilalx, adu duHKakekx biVja' eMdu heVLuvAga adakekx `suKavanunx sAdhisidare, adu duHKakekx kAraNavAgutatxde' eMbathaRvide. nAvu suKa paTaTx meVle adanunx matetx matetx paDeyabeVkeMba Ase uMTAgutatxde. adanunx paDeyuvavaregU namage duHKa (kaSaTx) uMTAgutatxde. atiyAda suKadiMda duHKa uMTAgabahudu:}
\ullekha{suKava nishecxYsalilalx, adu duHKakekx biVja. duHKava nishecxYsalilalx, suKadoDalu (savasaM. 9; suMkada. 622-196).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{subudidhxleVpagArxhaka maheVshavxra}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{maheVshavxra sathxladalilx sAdhakanu apupx eMba tananx aMgadalilxruva subudidhx eMba hasatxdiMda guruliMgada bAyiyAda jihevxge ruciyanunx apiRsutAtxne. aMdare tananx nAlageyalelxV avanu guruliMga\-vanunx sAthxpisikoMDiruvudariMda, avana nAlagege baruva ruci\-yelalxvU adaralilxruva guruliMgakekx apiRtavAdaMteyeV. hiVge maheVshavxranu tananx subudidhxyanunx leVpisikoMDu guru\-liMgavanunx garxhisuvudariMda avanu subudidhxleVpagArxhaka maheV\-shavxranenisikoLuLxtAtxne, hAgU avanu shivaliMgavAgutAtxne:}
\ullekha{guruliMgAMga subudidhxleVpagArxhaka maheVshavxra shivaliMgavAda (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 1412-504).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{sUtaka nAlukx}
\src{va}
\meaning{\artha{shabadxsUtaki: tamage elAlx gotutx eMdu heVLikoLuLxva ajAcnxnigaLu. balalxvaru balalxru elalxretatx balalxru?}
\ullekha{kUDalacenanxsaMgayayxnalilx shabadxsUtakigaLavaretatx balalxru? (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 645-194).}
\artha{liMgasUtaki: mAtumAtige liMgavenunxtatx adara mahatavx gotitxlalxdavanu:}
\ullekha{liMga liMgaveMbava liMgasUtakiyayayx, jaMgama jaMgamaveMbava jaMgamasUtakiyayayx. parxsAda parxsAda\-veM parxsAdasUtakiyayAyx I tirxvidhasUtakiya mAta keVLalAgadu (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 667-199).}
\artha{jaMgamasUtaki: nijavAda jaMgama yAru eMdu tiLiyadeyeV mAtumAtige jaMgama jaMgama enunxvavanu.}
\artha{parxsAdasUtaki: parxsAdada mahatavx gotitxlalxde A hesarinalilx padeV padeV AhAra, pAniVyagaLanunx sivxVkarisuvavanu.}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{hadinAlukx terana Bakitx}
\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{sAdhakanu tananx AdhAyxtimxka pathada pArxraMBika haMtadalilx jaMgamaliMgakekx hadinAlukx riVtiya Bakitxyanunx toVrisabeVku. rAjanobabxnige parxjeyu toVruva gwravavanenxV, Bakatxnu jaMgamanige toVrisutAtxne. I Bakitxyalilxruva hadinAlukx aMshagaLa vivara hiVgide:}}
\newmeaning{\artha{liMgakekx majajxna mADisabeVku.} \artha{vasatxrXdiMda adanunx oresabeVku;} \artha{liMgakekx gaMdhavanUnx;} \artha{akaSxteyanUnx leVpisabeVku;} \artha{paterx puSapxgaLanunx apiRsabeVku;} \artha{dhUpAratiyanUnx;} \artha{diVpAratiyanUnx beLagabeVku;} \artha{neYveVdayx mADabeVku;} \artha{niVranunx apiRsabeVku;} \artha{tAMbUlavanunx apiRsabeVku;} \artha{jaMgamaliMgakUkx suKAsana niVDabeVku;} \artha{jaMgamaliMgakekx maMtarx sotxVtarx giVta nataRnagaLu AgabeVku;} \artha{jaMgamaliMgakekx vasAtxrXlaMkAra, ABaraNagaLa dhAraNe mADabeVku;}
\artha{rAjanige hiMtirugalu vAhanada EpARDu mADuvaMte jaMgamaliMgakUkx vAhanada EpARTu mADabeVku;} \artha{Adare I vacanadalilx idAvudanUnx mADabAradu, ideVnanUnx mADadeyeV parxsAdavanunx paDedukoLuLxvavanige guruliMgajaMgama uMTu, uLidavarige ilalx eMdu heVLalAgide. liMga\-vanUnx jaMgamavanUnx obabx sAdhAraNa rAjanaMte kANabAradu eMbudAgide:} \ullekha{iMtiV hadinAlukx terada Bakitxyanu caraliMgaveMba jaMgamaliMgakekx dAsoVhava mADi parxsAdava koMba BakatxMge guruvuMTu, liMgavuMTu, jaMgamavuMTu, pAdoVdaka parxsAdavuMTu, AcAravuMTu, sadaBxkitxyuMTu. (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 1467-536).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\src{va}
\meaning{\arthanonum{1. ataLa, 2. vitaLa, 3. sutaLa, 4. rasAtaLa, 5. taLAtaLa, 6. mahAtaLa, 7. pAtALa, 8. BUloVka idara keLage; 9. BuvaloRVka, 10. savxloRVka, 11. mahaloRVka, 12. janaloRVka, 13. tapoVloVka matutx 14. satayx\-loVka I Aru BUloVkada meVle:}
\ullekha{Adi anAdi hadinAlukxloVka kAla kalipxta maMtarx taMtarx... obabx sharaNa Bakitxya mADutitxpupxda kaMDenayayx (savasaM. 2; alalxma. 881-261); IreVLu Buvana, hadinAlukxloVkadoDeya mikikxna mAtina jAcnxnigaLetatxbalalxru? (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 1197-414); amugeVshavxraliMgave, nimamx sharaNaru IreVLuBuvana hadinAlukxloVkadalilx liMga\-sahita opupxvaru. (savasaM. 5; amurA. 606-191); IreVLu BuvanaveMba hadinAlukx loVkaMgaLa dharisi ADutitxpaRvu. (savasaM. 8; bAciba. 202-80); IreVLu Buvanava hadinAlukx loVkavanoMdu iruve nuMgitutx noVDA. (savasaM. 10; jakakxNa. 1119-584).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{hodadxda parxpaMcika}
\meaning{\arthanonum{badalAgada parxpaMca. idu iMdirxyagoVcara parxpaMcakekx anavxyisade, adaroLage aMtasathxvAgiruva nitayxparatatatxvXkekx anavxyisutAtxne:}
\ullekha{I hodadxda parxpaMcikava nitayxda tatatxvXvanu madhayxmadalilx kaMDe kANA (savasaM. 4; sidadhxrA. 873-246).}}
\end{entry}
